<script>
  $(document).ready(function () {
    $(".early-access-subscription-toggle").on("click", function(e){
      toggleSubscription();
    })
  });

  const toggleSubscription = () => {
    $('[data-id="early-access-monthly"]').toggleClass('active');
    $('.early-access-subscription-monthly').toggleClass('d-none');
    $('[data-id="early-access-annually"]').toggleClass('active');
    $('.early-access-subscription-annual').toggleClass('d-none');
  }

  const focusAndOpenAnnualSubscription = () => {
    $('[data-id="early-access-monthly"]').removeClass('active');
    $('[data-id="early-access-annually"]').addClass('active');
    $(".monthly-package").addClass('d-none');
    $(".annual-package").removeClass('d-none');
    $(".annual-package .open-shopping-cart-button").click();
  }

  const focusAndOpenMonthlySubscription = () => {
    $('[data-id="early-access-annually"]').removeClass('active');

    $(".monthly-package").removeClass('d-none');

  }
</script>

      </h5>

      <img class="pr-2" src="https://d1zazrti94enmy.cloudfront.net/assets/icons/onboarding/listing/chevron-down-520ecc0a81449160731d295122d6dbf4301c1072fd2f27a104e4a40d111d9136.svg">
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<div id="collapse_8" class="collapse" aria-labelledby="heading_8" data-parent="#faq-accordion">
  <div class="mt-3">
    <p>When buying an online business, you take on all the responsibility for its growth and success. However, you'll purchase an established online company with a digital presence and customer base. Therefore, you should search online for the monthly traffic, revenue generation, and growth potential of any business you might buy.</p>

  </div>
</div>
<div id="heading_9">
  <hr>

  <div class="cursor-pointer ng-isolate-scope" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#collapse_9" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapse_9">
    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between">
      <h5>
        Why buy an online business?
      </h5>

      <img class="pr-2" src="https://d1zazrti94enmy.cloudfront.net/assets/icons/onboarding/listing/chevron-down-520ecc0a81449160731d295122d6dbf4301c1072fd2f27a104e4a40d111d9136.svg">
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<div id="collapse_9" class="collapse" aria-labelledby="heading_9" data-parent="#faq-accordion">
  <div class="mt-3">
    <p>Online businesses offer incredible scalability with relatively few overheads. With strategic SEO website design and digital marketing, you can turn your home-based passive income into solid revenue streams. Many legitimate businesses began as small side hustles. </p>

  </div>
</div>
<div id="heading_10">
  <hr>

  <div class="cursor-pointer ng-isolate-scope" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#collapse_10" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapse_10">

<div id="collapse_10" class="collapse" aria-labelledby="heading_10" data-parent="#faq-accordion">

Instead, we support people buying and selling a range of internet businesses, from blogs to SAAS companies, for a minimal fee. <div id="collapse_11" class="collapse" aria-labelledby="heading_11" data-parent="#faq-accordion">

  </div>

<div id="heading_12">

<div id="collapse_12" class="collapse" aria-labelledby="heading_12" data-parent="#faq-accordion">

You need to create an SEO-friendly website and invest in digital marketing. </p>

        How do I start an online business with no money?
      </h5>

      <img class="pr-2" src="https://d1zazrti94enmy.cloudfront.net/assets/icons/onboarding/listing/chevron-down-520ecc0a81449160731d295122d6dbf4301c1072fd2f27a104e4a40d111d9136.svg">

<div id="collapse_15" class="collapse" aria-labelledby="heading_15" data-parent="#faq-accordion">
  <div class="mt-3">
    <p>The best way to <a href="https://flippa.com/blog/how-to-start-an-e-commerce-business/">start an e-commerce business</a> with no start-up funds is to sell your services. However, you must create a website and promote your business to attract customers. Therefore, you may not make significant net profits at first. You'll need to invest your earnings into your business to grow and diversify your audience.</p>

  </div>

        How much does it cost to start an online shop?
      </h5>

      <img class="pr-2" src="https://d1zazrti94enmy.cloudfront.net/assets/icons/onboarding/listing/chevron-down-520ecc0a81449160731d295122d6dbf4301c1072fd2f27a104e4a40d111d9136.svg">
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<div id="collapse_16" class="collapse" aria-labelledby="heading_16" data-parent="#faq-accordion">
  <div class="mt-3">
    <p>E-commerce retailers have relatively few overheads when setting up an online shop. If you buy an established business, you'll need to pay one upfront fee and various costs to grow and maintain the business. Starting a business from scratch, you should expect to pay for branding, website building, SEO and marketing, stock, domain name, software, hosting, and SSL certificate.</p>

  </div>
